# FPV simulation model validation calculations

Generated: 2026-06-12

This report is generated by `docs/scripts/analyze_fpv_model_sources.py`. It fetches open internet sources, caches the raw files under `docs/data/raw`, and compares them with the current `DroneConfig` presets.

## High-signal findings

- The current `racingQuad` rotor coefficient is `1.450e-06` N/(rad/s)^2. UIUC 5-inch three-blade prop data averages `1.175e-06`, and Mini Quad Test Bench 5-inch FPV motor/prop rows average `1.487e-06`. That puts the current coefficient at `0.98x` of the FPV bench mean and `1.23x` of the UIUC 5-inch mean.
- With the current coefficient, `racingQuad` reaches `13.500` N per rotor at `29138` rpm. Using the Mini Quad Test Bench mean coefficient, the same thrust would require about `28773` rpm.
- The current `racingQuad` tip Mach at max thrust is `0.56`. Using FPV bench k for the same thrust and radius would put tip Mach near `0.55`.
- In cold sea-level air (`-10 C`), the same `racingQuad` max RPM reaches tip Mach `0.60` because speed of sound falls to `325.195` m/s. In a hot 3000 m case (`30 C`), standard-atmosphere density ratio is `0.658`, so the same-thrust RPM scale is `1.233x` before battery/motor limits.
- NACA/NASA propeller compressibility references put take-off/climb efficiency-loss onset around tip Mach `0.50..0.70` and serious losses for one high-speed two-blade prop above about `0.91`. The current `racingQuad` default/cold max Mach rows are `0.56`/`0.60`, with current compressibility thrust scale `0.962`/`0.936`; the onset magnitude is plausible, while the model is not near the serious-loss threshold.
- UIUC prop data uses `J = V/(nD)`, while this code's `rotorAdvanceRatio` is `mu = V/(omega R) = J/pi`. At `racingQuad` hover RPM and 12.5 m/s level forward speed, `J` is `0.453` and UIUC 5-inch fits predict CT/static CT near `0.543`, CP/static CP near `0.683`, and Q/T ratio `1.259`; the current airflow multiplier and same-RPM constant-Q/T power proxy are `1.063`, so forward-flow thrust and power rolloff are likely under-modeled if these quantities are intended to match prop data.
- The Tyto Windshaper lead packet adds an article-level dynamic forward-flow trend: a 9-inch propeller tested at `0..17 m/s` and 9000 RPM loses `75%` thrust while power drops only `19%` from 0 to 17 m/s. That endpoint is `J=0.496` / code `mu=0.158` for the 9-inch setup, close to the current `racingQuad` 12.5 m/s hover-RPM proxy `J=0.453`; it reinforces the UIUC warning that thrust can roll off strongly while power does not drop proportionally. It is still a lead/digitization target, not raw 5-inch CSV data.
- The IMAV 2021 RMIT source packet adds the best direct 5-inch forward-flow lead so far: 5-inch, 3-blade HQProp V1S propellers, T-Motor F80 2500kv, `10/15/20 m/s` wind, `30..90 deg` flow angles, and RCBenchmark thrust/torque/RPM/power instrumentation. Its cropped high-quality region covers `J=0.157..0.630`, overlapping current `racingQuad` hover/max RPM proxies. The companion figure-inventory packet extracts `8` embedded PDF images and marks `18` Figs. 5-8 panels for `eta(RPM)` digitization. It intentionally does not fit CT/CP because the public figures are propulsive-efficiency curves, not raw thrust/torque coefficient tables.
- The Kolaei 2018 inflow-angle rotor packet adds a same-definition `mu = V/(Omega*R)` check for forward-flow and transverse-flow behavior. It reports `CT`, `CP`, and roll-moment coefficient trends for 11-inch and 18-inch rotors at `3000/4000/5000 rpm`, inflow angles `90..-90 deg`, and `mu` up to about `0.30`. Current `racingQuad` hover-RPM `mu` is `0.144` at `12.5 m/s` and `0.231` at `20 m/s`, so the source overlaps the main forward-flight band, but it is larger-rotor evidence and should not overwrite 5-inch FPV coefficient scale. Figs. 9-11 are now listed as pending CT/CP/CMx digitization targets.
- A low-precision digitization of Stanford STARMAC II Fig. 9 gives measured rotor flapping deflection of about `1.12` deg at `3.4` m/s wind; the current `racingQuad` same-speed hover proxy gives `0.27` deg. Treat this as a flapping-scale sanity check only; tune against advance ratio and rotor stiffness before using it as a direct fit.
- Current blade-dissymmetry uses `mu=0.08..0.34` for lift dissymmetry and `mu=0.42..0.82` for retreating-blade stall. NASA high-advance-ratio rotor references cover operation up to about `mu=1.0`, and the DLR dynamic-stall validation paper uses model-rotor data at `mu=0.4`. `racingQuad` at hover RPM reaches `mu=0.346` at 30 m/s and `mu=0.462` at 40 m/s, while max RPM at 40 m/s is only `mu=0.206`; the stall threshold is plausible as a high-speed/low-RPM edge, but UIUC 5-inch prop data do not extend far enough to validate this RBS curve directly.
- The low-Reynolds proxy is currently a small-prop feature: `racingQuad` max low-Re loss remains `0.000` in the hot 3000 m case because the 5-inch radius gates it out, while `cinewhoop` reaches `1.000` max-loss proxy under the same density/temperature.
- UIUC 5-inch static rows give a Re75-proxy sweep of roughly `3745-25080` over the tested RPM range, with mean high/low-Re CT ratio `1.137`. The current `racingQuad` hot-3000m max Re75 proxy is `47944`, inside/above that UIUC 5-inch static band, so a zero low-Re loss for 5-inch racing props is defensible while the smaller `cinewhoop` still needs the loss path.
- A hover momentum-theory wake time proxy gives `R/vi = 0.0068 s` and `2R/vi = 0.0136 s` for `racingQuad`. The configured `rotor_inflow_tau = 0.0350 s` is `5.1x` the one-radius wake transit time and `2.6x` the disk-diameter transit time, so it is a damped/gameplay-friendly wake lag rather than a bare momentum transit constant.
- Adding PX4's Typhoon H480 hexacopter model gives a heavier open-source thrust-margin anchor: mass `2.020` kg, six `0.128 m` rotors, `maxRotVelocity=1500` rad/s, and derived max `T/W=5.83` with hover at `0.414` of max speed. Current `hexLift` max `T/W=3.79` is `0.65x` the PX4 Typhoon margin, and its max rotor speed is `0.57x` the Typhoon max; keep large-rotor presets separate from 5-inch FPV RPM assumptions.
- For the HQ v1s 5x4x3 bench rows, fitted motor current is approximately `I = 1.430 * T^1.158` where `T` is per-motor thrust in newtons. This estimates racing hover current near `18.039` A for four motors before avionics.
- At the current `racingQuad` battery resistance of 0.018 ohm, the fitted hover current implies about `0.325` V pack sag. The 90 A current limit implies `10.807` N per rotor on the fitted HQ prop curve, below the configured `13.500` N per rotor.
- The ZJU ground-effect/motor-calibration source reports single-rotor `k_T = 4.008e-08` N/rpm^2, which converts to `3.655e-06` N/(rad/s)^2, with `Q/T = 0.0159` m. The `Q/T` value is close to this project's 5-inch yaw torque order of magnitude.
- Applying the ZJU paper's additional-thrust formula at the current `racingQuad` physical clearance gives `h/R=1.0` thrust multiplier `1.332` versus the current model's `1.144`; the current extra thrust is `0.43x` the ZJU formula extra at that height. ZJU also reports 0.1 m / 2.0 m rotor-drag ratios of `dx=0.596` and `dy=0.618`, below the `0.949` sqrt-thrust prediction, so the current added near-ground drag should not be treated as the same physical coefficient without a separate fit.
- The new near-surface and wall-obstruction packets tie ground, ceiling, and wall rows together while separating ideal disk overlap, dirty-air thrust loss, and wall-attraction force. For `racingQuad` at a flat wall `d/R=0.25`, the runtime mapping gives `2.05%` equivalent vehicle thrust loss for two affected rotors and `0.063x` weight wall force; at `d/R=1.0`, ideal disk overlap is zero and the side-flow heuristic gives only `0.58%` loss with `0.032x` weight wall force. Published sidewall anchors report total lift change below `5%` and negligible total-thrust wall effect, so tune wall proximity mostly as attraction/moment/dirty-air handling unless stronger total-thrust data is found.
- The A4MC source-quality response packet turns the synthetic wall-skim gate into a `17649`-row matrix. The reference `confidence=0.86`, fresh, `shelter=0.74`, `shear=0.58/block`, `source_turbulence=0.24`, `updraft=0.18 m/s` case adopts quality `0.86`, source turbulence `0.206`, natural turbulence proxy `0.786`, unstable mixed-ABL Dryden proxy `0.890` with vertical time-scale `0.627x`, stable mixed-ABL proxy `0.499` with vertical time-scale `1.243x`, source-gust Y peak proxy `0.409 m/s`, updraft target/1 s settled values `0.078/0.077 m/s`, terrain-vector peak proxy `0.192 m/s`, and ventilation efficiency `0.873`; a stale `160 tick` source drops the transient forcing to zero. The dedicated updraft/downwash sweep adds `385` scenarios across trust, confidence, freshness, local-voxel availability, ABL mixing, and raw vertical flow. The new pressure sweep adds `325` scenarios that mirror quality-gated A4MC pressure anomaly into density, barometer pressure, and local L2 static-port bias: the wall-skim `-12 Pa` raw anomaly becomes `-0.1032 hPa` barometer delta and `0.586 m` steady static-port altitude error, half confidence gives `0.341 m`, `-220 Pa` saturates at `0.65 m`, coarse flow gives `0 m`, and stale `+4500 Pa` returns density to `1.0x`. Runtime blackbox keeps the adopted A4MC source gust, signed updraft, terrain-shear, and pressure channels separate so source-quality tuning can distinguish coherent gust, vertical air mass, voxel terrain response, and atmospheric pressure response.
- The A4MC disk-gradient response packet adds a `6227`-row current-formula surface for rotor disk-gradient tuning. In the direct-core hover probe, `0.33 m/s` adopted pressure-gradient wind remains `0.33 m/s` once source quality is available, while source quality `0` disables the channel; the value sits below the `racingQuad` flapping/thrust-loss start thresholds of `0.312/0.485 m/s` adopted gradient and produces only `0.00018 deg` tilt. The full `12 m/s` max-spin sweep reaches `4.5 deg` tilt and `3.77%` thrust loss. The Fabric local-voxel coupling packet separately audits the bridge preprocessing that maps a one-sided `220 Pa` pressure step to `0.0801 m/s` before core disk-gradient response, and now adds `54` pressure-center scenarios for the core body-scale moment path: the offline wall-skim proxy moves the center by only `0.286 mm`, while strong one-sided wall+pressure signals hit the bounded `24 mm` offset and quality `0` disables the path. Runtime blackbox rows now expose the separated A4MC pressure-gradient wind contribution and the separated disk-gradient thrust-loss/load/vibration/stall response components alongside the total disk-gradient magnitude, so those packet surfaces can be compared to flight traces without mixing them into generic rotor load or vibration fields.
- The JIRS 2024 supplementary packet adds direct force/torque measurements: `225` parsed CSV rows plus `40` direct MAT uncertainty rows. With `100 cm` same-PWM rows as far baselines, closest ground rows at `h/R=0.328..0.394` have median/max Fz ratios `1.291x/1.315x`, closest ceiling rows have `1.227x/1.289x`, and wall rows over `d/R=0.965..3.0` have max absolute wall force/moment `0.4278 N` / `0.1195 N*m`. Use wall rows as signed attraction/moment evidence, not pure thrust-loss evidence, and weight terraXcube and DU2SRI wall rows separately because their direct wall-force uncertainty medians differ by about `28.5x`.
- The JIRS 2024 curve-fit packet converts the raw surface rows into conservative distance curves. At `h/R=1`, fitted ground and ceiling multipliers are `1.0856x` and `1.0961x`; current `racingQuad` is `1.054x` and `1.016x` those fitted multipliers. The cleanest wall fit is terraXcube absolute force (`R2=0.923`, `0.1077 N` at `d/R=1`), while pooled wall force is weak (`R2=0.225`, `0.1655 N` at `d/R=1`); current two-rotor wall force at `d/R=1` is `2.11x` that pooled fit.
- For `racingQuad`, hover induced velocity is `9.322` m/s. The code's VRS intensity band covers roughly `4.195-20.974` m/s descent, while the Cambridge dual-rotor paper reports strongest loss around `1.2-1.3 vi` (`11.186-12.118` m/s for this preset).
- The generated VRS/propwash scan now mirrors the current Java formula: `racingQuad` reaches `32.96%` max-spin VRS mean thrust loss at `1.2 vi`. Cambridge reports peak losses up to about one third, so the current mean-loss cap is essentially on that anchor.
- Shetty/Selig's small-prop VRS time histories report peak thrust fluctuations of about `+/-30%` near the minimum-thrust advance ratio; the current `racingQuad` logged VRS buffet envelope is `27.9%` at `1.2 vi`, just under that text anchor.
- A low-precision manual digitization of Shetty/Selig Figs. 11-13 puts the largest measured-limit half-amplitude near `66%` of mean CT at `J=-0.30`, mapping to about `1.24 vi`. The current `racingQuad` max-spin VRS buffet envelope at that same `V/vi` proxy is `27.9%`, or `0.42x` of the measured-limit envelope. Treat this as a min/max envelope comparison, not an RMS/statistical fit.
- The 2026 Physics of Fluids side-by-side propeller VRS source adds adjacent-rotor coupling evidence: side-by-side onset is `DR=0.9` versus isolated `DR=1.1`, tight `0.1R` co-rotating outer-vortex radius/circulation is `0.69x/0.66x` isolated, and current `racingQuad` adjacent disk-tip gap is `2.01R`, outside the tested `0.1..1.0R` gap range.
- The new VRS/propwash calibration packet makes the tuning surfaces one-table accessible. For `racingQuad`, the VRS active scan spans `0.75..1.90 vi`, propwash is fully active from `0.95 vi`, peak hover-spin loss is `17.4%`, max-spin buffet half-amplitude is `27.9%`, and propwash max torque is `0.035 N*m`. Keep VRS mean thrust loss, buffet, lateral disturbance, and propwash torque as separate surfaces.
- `racingQuad` battery IR is `4.500` mOhm/cell by the inferred `4S` pack. That sits in the high-C LiPo plausibility range, but max-current sag still reaches `1.620` V at the configured limit.
- A structured MQTB HQ v1s 5x4x3 current/power fit is now generated in `docs/data/mqtb_hq5x4x3_current_model_reference.csv`. The current fit has log-space R2 `0.9946` and RMS current residual `10.8%`. Projected through current `racingQuad`, hover is `18.039` A total, the 90 A pack limit maps to `10.807` N per motor, and the configured `13.500` N per motor would draw `116.449` A total (`1.29x` the pack current limit) on this representative prop curve.
- Against the same-cell public pack `Tattu R-Line V5 1550mAh 4S 150C`, `racingQuad` capacity is `0.97x` and current limit is `0.39x` of the listed continuous-current spec. But if the current preset's `4.500` mOhm/cell resistance were used at that reference pack's continuous current, sag would be `24.9%` of nominal voltage, so C-rating and ESR must be calibrated separately.
- Adding public FPV 4S charger-IR measurements gives under-20-cycle pack means from `4.975` to `6.850` mOhm/cell. `racingQuad`'s `4.5` mOhm/cell is `0.90x` the lowest measured row (`Acehe Formula 4S 95C 1500mAh`), so treat it as an aggressive fresh high-performance pack value, not a generic FPV LiPo. Versus the measured `Tattu 4S 45C 1550mAh` row it is `0.69x`, with measured-row sag `2.349` V at the current 90 A limit.
- The new APdrone battery-resistance envelope gives scale-sensitive log proxies for `apDrone()`'s `0.016 ohm` pack R. Hardware/capacity-supported current-scale choices imply `0.0194..0.0234 ohm` (`4.84..5.85 mOhm/cell`), so current `0.016 ohm` is plausible but low: `0.68..0.83x` of those proxies and `0.58..0.80x` of the Oscar 4S measured-IR rows.
- A new LiPo ESR method table adds temperature/SOC guardrails and the conservative IR-based `true C = 2500 / sqrt(capacity_mAh * highest_cell_IR_mOhm)` check. Using configured mean cell IR as a proxy, `racingQuad` lands at `30.43 C / 45.64 A`, so its `90 A` limit is `1.97x` that continuous-current guardrail; `apDrone()` lands at `32.27 C / 48.41 A`, so its `150 A` limit is `3.10x`. If a 10 C drop roughly doubles IR, those ratios rise to `2.79x` and `4.38x`.
- The new Mendeley C-rate/temperature packet inventories `334` files and parses a `33`-curve subset. At `2C`, 5 C versus 25 C capacity ratios are `0.616` for NCA, `0.830` for NMC, and `0.893` for LFP; LFP `20C` at 25 C heats by `35.0 C`, while the selected 5 C row collapses to `0.0045x` the 25 C capacity. This supports strong cold/high-C limiting shape, but the dataset is cylindrical Li-ion, not FPV pouch-pack absolute ESR.
- The APdrone drag calibration packet now condenses open-field speed-envelope, dynamics, and trim/deceleration filters. `apDrone()` X drag-limited speed is `20.99 m/s`, while `racingQuad()` X is `17.03 m/s`; APdrone's `18.72 m/s` GPS max is feasible for `apDrone()` but not `racingQuad()` under the current level-flight drag check. The fastest straight-ish decel filter has only `3` events and a zero-thrust diagnostic coefficient of `0.00841 N/(m/s)^2` (`0.069x` `apDrone()` X), so do not fit `CdA` directly from these logs.
- The APdrone powertrain calibration packet now gathers APdrone motor-PDF rows, Foxeer Donut 5145 public image data, selected Tyto static tests, Tyto torque fits, and MQTB current-shape rows. Current `apDrone()` max rotor thrust is `0.953..1.122x` the visible APdrone PDF prop maxima; the 4S loaded-RPM estimate brackets current `k` at `0.761..1.075x`; the closest public Foxeer Donut image point gives `k` ratio `1.000x`, max-RPM ratio `0.998x`, and max-thrust ratio `0.996x`. The exact YSIDO 2507 + Donut 5145 curve is still missing, but the current static thrust/RPM scale is well supported.
- The Tyto 5-inch public static scan is now a broader `racingQuad` static-prop sanity packet. `docs/data/tyto_5in_static_prop_packet.csv` parses `28` 5-inch candidate propellers, `89` public tests, and `1548` static samples. The median per-test static `T/omega^2` is `1.3924e-6 N/(rad/s)^2`, or `0.960x` current `racingQuad.k`, so the static coefficient scale is well supported. However, no parsed Tyto 5-inch test reaches the current `13.5 N` per-rotor thrust ceiling; the strongest parsed test is `12.55 N` (`0.929x` current max). This packet has no airspeed/wind-speed column and must not be used as forward-flow calibration.
- The current battery temperature model raises `racingQuad` pack resistance to `2.01x` and cuts max-current scale to `0.73x` at 0 C. At 70 C, resistance is `1.07x`, current scale `0.83x`, and thermal power limit `0.78x`; this matches the qualitative Li-ion/LiPo pattern that cold mainly hurts power delivery and heat drives protection.
- A Jeffco Aeromodlers RC LiPo ESR temperature test on 3S 1000mAh packs gives paired 71F-to-42F total-IR ratios of `1.68..2.03x` across ESR Meter/iCharger rows. The current model gives `1.52x` for the same warm/cold pair, only `0.75..0.91x` of those field measurements, so cold ESR growth is likely conservative for small LiPo packs.
- CALCE low-current OCV data at 25 C gives median `3.665` V/cell at 50% SOC; the current `racingQuad` OCV curve gives `3.822` V/cell (`15.288` V pack). At SOC 0.50 and 90 A load, the current steady sag mirror gives `1.999` V total sag and `13.747` V bus voltage before thermal dynamics. NASA B0005 first-cycle loaded discharge is `3.546` V/cell at the same SOC under about 2 A load. At low reserve, CALCE 25 C medians are `3.463` V/cell at 10% SOC and `3.423` V/cell at 5%, while the current 4.2/3.3 V code curve gives `3.552` and `3.453` V/cell.
- The SOC power limiter is intentionally a reserve cliff: `racingQuad` at 4% SOC has OCV `13.748` V, SOC power limit `0.350`, fresh SOC-resistance scale `1.311x`, and at the 90 A load scan the combined power limit is `0.350`.
- CALCE SP20-2 DST pulse data at 25 C shows post-discharge rest recovery on a slow relaxation scale: 50/80% SOC 63%-recovery times are `630`/`79` s, with 10 s sample spacing. Current `racingQuad` sag recovery tau is `0.750` s, so it should be interpreted as a short electrical sag term, not as long Li-ion polarization/hysteresis recovery.
- The extracted Mendeley LP-503562-IS-3 ECM fit summary has `57` fitted-cycle files across `5` packs. Mean fitted `RO` spans `75.586-92.987` mOhm/cell; the new SOC/SOH lookup makes fresh low-SOC `RO` about `1.033x` fresh high-SOC, while worn (`SOH<0.75`) low-SOC rows reach `1.190x`. Use this for resistance shape, not FPV high-C absolute ESR.
- Projecting that Mendeley `RO(SOC,SOH)` shape onto the current `racingQuad` absolute ESR changes pack resistance from `18.048` mOhm at fresh/full to `21.425` mOhm at worn/10% SOC. At the configured `90` A limit, sag rises from `1.624` V to `1.928` V; that 90 A limit is `0.57x` of the row's 20%-nominal-sag current.
- `docs/data/fpv_lipo_esr_calibration_packet.csv` is now the first-stop handoff for battery ESR tuning. It mirrors `774` `fpv_lipo_esr_packet_*` rows and keeps the policy explicit: anchor absolute room-condition ESR to FPV charger-IR rows (`4.975..6.850 mOhm/cell`), use Mendeley LiPo ECM only for SOC/SOH shape, use C-rate/temperature plus Jeffco rows only for limiter/temperature shape, and never infer ESR directly from manufacturer C-rating.
- Parsing the NASA Li-ion aging impedance zip adds `1956` EIS rows across `34` 18650 cells. Room-temperature worn (`SOH<0.75`) rows have median `Re` scale `1.224x` and `Re+Rct` scale `1.397x` versus room high-SOH; use it as an aging-shape cross-check, not FPV absolute ESR. Hot high-SOH 43 C rows have median `Re` scale `0.657x` versus room high-SOH.
- A 2026 Figshare high-current EIS dataset adds `6` BAK N18650CNP cells cycled for `400` cycles at `4.0C` discharge and `1.6C` charge, with EIS every cycle from `0.05` Hz to `50000` Hz. This is a strong high-current impedance-aging source, but still an 18650 Li-ion shape prior rather than FPV LiPo absolute ESR.
- Parsing the Figshare MAT summary arrays adds `6` cells x `400` high-current cycle rows. Median last10/first10 summary-IR growth is `1.051x` with median capacity SOH `0.808` after 400 cycles at `4.0C` discharge, a useful aging-shape prior for current-limit/sag degradation.
- `racingQuad.motor_tau` is `0.0450` s, about `3.60x` RotorS/PX4 `timeConstantUp` and `1.80x` `timeConstantDown`. That is defensible if it includes ESC/load/voltage effects, but it is slower than the simple open-source actuator lag reference.
- The inferred `racingQuad` motor scale is about `2341` rpm/V with `Kt=0.0041` N*m/A. At configured max thrust, back-EMF leaves `0.259` full-drive voltage headroom and the 75%-efficiency shaft-power current proxy is `45.769` A per motor, `2.03x` the configured per-motor battery-current budget.
- MQTB's FPV-class Emax Eco 2306 row reports tested KV `2300` rpm/V, mass `29.700` g, stator `23x6` mm, and an `40` A ESC test setup. Current `racingQuad` inferred KV is `1.02x` that tested KV, and its per-motor current limit is `0.56x` the MQTB ESC rating, so the electrical class is FPV-plausible even though thermal rise still needs direct temperature data.
- The Mendeley/Tyto 30-inch hover thrust-stand packet adds open raw Flight Stand data for static curve/noise checks: `docs/data/mendeley_30in_prop_stand_packet.csv` has `3593` rows mirrored as `mendeley_30in_prop_packet_*`, backed by `35` raw 100 Hz `.xls` files and `20` summary workbooks. Across P1..P5, no-intercept `T=k*omega^2` fits span `6.69e-4..8.47e-4 N/(rad/s)^2` with R2 `0.99956..0.99985`; raw-file RPM CV median is `0.136%`, thrust CV median `0.821%`, and median `Q/T` is `0.03899 m`. These coefficients are `462..584x` `racingQuad` and `14.9..18.8x` `heavyLift`, so use them as large-prop/static-test schema and measurement-noise anchors, not FPV tuning constants.
- With `motorActiveBrakingStrength=0.55`, a zero-command braking proxy at `racingQuad` max RPM is `29.333` A and `0.120` N*m per motor, while the braking response tau proxy is `14.062` ms. Treat this as an ESC-electrical stress model until matched to blackbox current/RPM decel traces.
- `docs/data/motor_response_dynamics_packet.csv` now gathers RotorS/PX4 lag rows, Betaflight PR #12562 RPM slews, APdrone urban eRPM command/RPM lag, AI-IO hover-RPM scale, and current ESC/braking proxies into 210 `motor_response_packet_*` rows. PR #12562's strongest 50 ms positive slew is `503271` rpm/s (`0.78x` current `racingQuad.maxRPM/motor_tau`), while strongest negative slew is `525478` rpm/s (`0.254x` current braking proxy), so spin-up is same-order but active braking is much stronger than observed logs.
- APdrone urban eRPM logs give command/RPM level-lag P50 `47.9` ms and delta-lag P50 `39.9` ms, but weak first-order tau P50 across files is only `3.95` ms. Current `apDrone.motorTimeConstantSeconds = 15` ms is `3.80x` that first-order tau and `0.31x` the level-lag P50, so command/log alignment lag and physical motor response should stay separate in future tuning.
- `docs/data/wavelab_pelican_motor_response_packet.csv` adds 54 WAVELab Pelican flights with 100 Hz actual and commanded motor-speed fields. It gives command-to-actual derivative lag P50/P90 of `30/50 ms`; after a static command-to-actual map, first-order tau P10/P50/P90 is `0.182/0.320/1.031 s`, with P50 `7.11x` current `racingQuad.motor_tau`. Because the source uses AscTec integer motor units and a 5-sample smoothing filter, treat it as a system-ID timing envelope, not FPV mechanical-RPM or ESC-step truth.
- `racingQuad.rotorInertia` is `5.376e-06` kg*m^2, equivalent to `4.000` g under a uniform 5-inch blade proxy. Official HQProp/Gemfan 5-inch tri-blade masses make the current inertia `0.88..1.05x` their uniform-blade estimate and the equivalent mass `0.89..1.05x` their listed mass, so the preset is low for prop-only inertia unless mass is intentionally hub-biased or scaled for response.
- NASA multicopter blade-deflection measurements put DJI Phantom 3 prop coning near `1.95` deg and `4.080` mm at 8500 rpm. Current `racingQuad` coning is an intensity proxy, not an angle, but max-steady target intensity `0.639` only removes `2.43%` thrust. Its arm-flex max-snap proxy gives `5.940` mm vertical tip deflection and `2.08` deg thrust-axis tilt; simple 5-inch carbon-arm beam cases span `1.866..11.716` mm at max thrust and `28..69` Hz first-bending frequency, so the current flex magnitude is plausible for a thin/flexible arm but high for a stiff arm.
- `RotorSpec.defaultBladePitchMeters(radius)` gives `P=1.70R`, so every current preset without an override uses `P/D=0.85`. That matches same-size 5-inch racing prop pitch within `0.85..1.18x`, but `heavyLift`'s 10-inch effective pitch is `1.70..1.89x` official Gemfan 1045/1050 pitch, so heavy-lift pitch-speed, windmilling, chord/Re proxy, and stall geometry should not inherit the 5-inch default blindly.
- UIUC geometry TXT rows add actual `r/R, c/R, beta` station data. At 70%R, `racingQuad`'s chord proxy is `0.58..0.89x` same-size UIUC 5-inch chord and its pitch angle is `1.01..1.22x`; `heavyLift`'s current angle is `1.18..1.86x` UIUC 10-inch references, with local P/D `1.19..1.92x`.
- `docs/data/prop_pitch_geometry_packet.csv` now mirrors 294 `prop_pitch_packet_*` rows into the global summary. The packet keeps current presets, official prop references, UIUC 70%R summaries, current-vs-official ratios, and current-vs-UIUC ratios in one handoff table; the summary rows make the tuning split explicit: `racingQuad` default pitch is acceptable as a 5-inch proxy, while 10-inch lift presets need explicit blade-pitch/chord geometry.
- The new APC high-advance packet extends axial propeller coverage beyond UIUC's `J ~= 0.57` limit: 7 APC files produce `7590` rows up to `J = 2.466` / equivalent code `mu = 0.785`. Moderate 5-inch props still lose positive axial CT around equivalent `mu = 0.345..0.360`; only high-pitch axial props cover the current `mu = 0.42` retreating-stall start. Use this to separate axial high-J prop behavior from edgewise high-mu rotor stall evidence.
- `docs/data/mejzlik_wind_tunnel_prop_packet.csv` adds a measured high-`J` axial prop table from the AirShaper/Mejzlik wind-tunnel study. Wind-tunnel `CT` remains positive at `J=0.6` (`0.0411`) and is negative at `J=0.8` (`-0.0035`), giving a linear `CT=0` boundary near `J=0.784` / code `mu=0.250`. At `racingQuad` hover RPM that maps to about `21.62 m/s`, while the current high-advance-loss start maps to `J=1.445` / about `39.84 m/s`; use this as an axial windmilling check, not a direct edgewise retreating-blade-stall fit.
- `cinewhoop.rotorInertia` maps to `18.698` g under the same uniform-blade proxy. Against official 3-inch/D90 prop mass rows, its configured inertia is `5.8..12.6x` the prop-only uniform estimate, so treat it as duct/fan/motor/gameplay inertia unless measured ducted-rotor inertia supports it.
- The U8/Kv100 open dyno processed maps reach `57.692` C max reported temperature and `484.167` W max loss in the 36 V map. Current `racingQuad` starts motor limiting at `95` C and cuts to the minimum thermal scale by `125` C; its full-power no-airspeed proxy steady motor rise is `178.571` C above ambient, so sustained full throttle should thermally limit.
- `docs/data/motor_thermal_packet.csv` now mirrors 240 `motor_thermal_packet_*` rows into the global summary, separating U8 dyno temperature/loss evidence, MQTB FPV 2306 hardware metadata, current electrical stress, current thermal proxies, and copper resistance scaling. At 25 C ambient, `racingQuad` full-power motor proxy reaches `203.6` C (`2.55x` the limit margin and `1.79x` the cutoff margin), while the ESC proxy reaches `117.6` C (`0.975x` cutoff margin); read this as a sustained-abuse limiter check, not a measured FPV temperature trace.
- The current copper winding coefficient `0.0039 / C` gives resistance scales of `1.39x` at 125 C and `1.60x` at 180 C. That supports the direction of hot-winding torque/current loss, though actual FPV motor winding temperature needs telemetry or bench data.
- `coaxialX8` has upper/lower rotor spacing `z/D = 0.72`, inside the New Dexterity/Hackaday second 11-inch local-efficiency region (`0.70..0.85`). Mirroring the current wake model with zero crossflow gives lower-rotor wake thrust scale `0.930` at hover and `0.810` at max spin, so the model predicts about `7.0%`/`19.0%` lower-rotor thrust loss at that spacing.
- Parsing the open New Dexterity `Data.rar` raw CSVs confirms the 11-inch mechanical-efficiency shape: at 1500 g pair thrust, equal-command `z/D=0.70` reconstructs `7.16` g/W_mech versus `6.95` g/W_mech at `z/D=0.55`. The current wake model changes only from `7.0%` to `7.1%` hover loss across those points, so it captures a loss magnitude but not the measured local efficiency valley.
- The same raw 11-inch `z/D=0.70` data shows optimal-fit unequal commands improve reconstructed mechanical efficiency by `5.1%` at 1000 g pair thrust, using a right/left PWM ratio near `1.32x`. Equal upper/lower commands should therefore be treated as a baseline, not an efficiency optimum, for X8 modeling.
- Extending the same raw archive across usable 11/16.2/22 inch full-range groups at 60% of each group's common equal-command max thrust, the largest measured mechanical-efficiency spread over `z/D` is `5.6%` for `11.0in 910kv 11V propdrivev2`: best `z/D=0.25`, worst `z/D=0.10`. The current hover wake-loss best-minus-worst delta is `5.7` percentage points, so the smooth wake-loss formula does not preserve the measured efficiency ordering.
- The strongest 60%-load optimal-fit command benefit found in the multi-size raw files is `11.6%` mechanical-efficiency gain for `22.0in 240kv 25V MN501S T` at `z/D=0.40`. This gives a direct allocation-surface target for future X8 mixer/efficiency modeling.
- Looking directly at each raw 10x10 command map near 60% load, the best mechanical-efficiency envelope point improves over equal-command interpolation by `9.4%` for `22.0in 240kv 25V MN501S T` at `z/D=1.00`, with electrical-efficiency delta `-0.0%` and right/left PWM ratio near `1.46x`. This is a raw-map allocation target independent of the precomputed optimal-fit files, and it keeps mechanical and electrical efficiency separate.
- Interpolating the raw command-map envelope to the current `coaxialX8` spacing (`z/D=0.72`) gives a runtime lookup target: at 60% normalized load, `22.0in 240kv 25V MN501S T` recommends right/left PWM ratio `1.45x`, with `6.9%` mechanical-efficiency gain and `0.9%` electrical-efficiency delta versus equal command.
- The smoothed `coaxialX8` runtime-allocation prior uses the nearest measured prop-diameter group `11.0in 910kv 11V propdrivev2` because the simulated diameter is `9.1 in`, below the measured 11-inch minimum. At 60% normalized load it recommends right/left PWM ratio `1.33x` and left/right scales `0.83/1.10` versus equal command; all-group ratio bounds are `1.22..1.45`.
- `docs/data/coaxial_allocation_calibration_packet.csv` now collects the full coaxial handoff surface into one narrow metric table and mirrors 835 `coaxial_packet_*` rows into the global summary. Treat it as an allocation/mixer prior: the benchmark right/left convention still needs mapping to project upper/lower rotor ordering and command limits before runtime use.
- Cubic command-surface fits over the New Dexterity 10x10 maps are usable for model fitting: total thrust has train/CV median RMSE `0.72%`/`1.07%` of map range across `29` fits, with median CV R2 `0.9979`; mechanical power has train/CV median RMSE `0.79%`/`1.24%` and median CV R2 `0.9972`. Prefer fitting thrust/power/torque surfaces, then derive efficiency, rather than fitting noisy g/W directly.
- `racingQuad` radius of gyration is `rx/ry/rz = 0.104/0.138/0.113` m, with yaw-axis inertia about `1.62x` the roll/pitch-axis mean. That is close to RotorS Hummingbird/PX4 Iris scale after mass normalization, so the base inertia order looks plausible.
- `racingQuad` runtime base drag at 10 m/s is `2.050` N on body X and `2.250` N on body Z before separated-flow additions, equal to `0.19x` and `0.21x` vehicle weight. The old `18.25`/`18.45` N values were a linear-as-quadratic projection guard, not runtime force.
- The IMAV 2022 quadrotor drag fit gives a mass-matched `racingQuad` low-speed linear drag coefficient of `0.201` N/(m/s), or `2.007` N at 10 m/s. Runtime X/Z drag at 10 m/s is `1.02x`/`1.12x` that mass-fit reference, with speed-specific equivalent CdA `0.033`/`0.037` m^2.
- Low-precision digitization of NASA Fig. 30 bare-airframe wind-tunnel drag gives a small-quad 0 deg median `Drag/q` of `0.225 ft^2` (`CdA 0.021 m^2`). Runtime `racingQuad` X-axis equivalent CdA at 10 m/s is `0.033 m^2`, or `1.60x` that bare-frame median. This remains a lower-bound body-drag anchor because it excludes powered rotor/body interaction.
- Low-precision digitization of NASA Figs. 18/20/22 powered full-airframe drag at `q=0.48 lb/ft^2`, yaw/pitch 0 deg gives a mid-RPM small-quad median of `1.601` N at `6.126` m/s (`CdA 0.070 m^2`). Runtime `racingQuad` X-axis base drag at the same speed is `1.196` N, `0.75x` that powered wind-tunnel median.
- The matching NASA powered lift plots, Figs. 17/19/21, give a mid-RPM small-quad median lift of `15.257` N at median `5400` RPM, about `1.14x` Table 1 nominal flight weight with total CT `0.012`. Per-rotor effective `k` is about `1.170e-05` N/(rad/s)^2. Current `racingQuad` uses `k=1.450e-06`, so at the same RPM it produces only `0.12x` the NASA median lift; matching that lift would need about `15488` RPM, `1.19x` current hover RPM. This is a prop-scale sanity check, not a direct 5-inch fit.
- Matching the same IMAV `racingQuad` 10 m/s reference with this project's runtime force law needs a body-X coefficient near `0.00207 N/(m/s)^2` if the shared `linearDragCoefficient = 0.18 N/(m/s)` is kept. The current X body coefficient is `0.0025`, so the IMAV low-speed target is reachable without treating the linear term as a quadratic CdA coefficient.
- UZH/RPG's FPV rotor-drag controller uses mass-normalized horizontal `k_drag_x/y = 0.544/0.386 1/s`. Mapping RPG x/y to this project's horizontal X/Z, the 10 m/s `racingQuad` linear-rotor-drag forces are `5.984`/`4.246` N, while runtime X/Z forces are `2.050`/`2.250` N, or `0.34x`/`0.53x` the RPG-derived reference.
- ICAS 2020 CFD reports `1.076` N drag for a 1.4 kg quadrotor in `10.7` m/s forward flight. Runtime `racingQuad` X-axis base drag at the same speed is `2.212` N, `2.1x` that CFD value; its vertical drag-only terminal-speed estimate is `41.132` m/s versus the ICAS no-prop freefall `29.310` m/s.
- UZH-FPV's public SplitS1 racing sequence reports peak speed `26.790` m/s (`96.4 km/h`). At that speed runtime `racingQuad` X-axis drag is `6.62` N, `0.13x` its level-flight horizontal thrust margin; required total thrust is `0.23x` configured max. Base drag no longer blocks the speed envelope, so remaining racing-speed calibration should focus on prop unloading, attitude, controller limits, and residual aero.
- Race Against the Machine adds an open-design 5-inch racing-quad log source with 36 flights, 500 Hz synchronized CSVs, thrust commands, battery voltage, IMU, motion-capture pose/velocity, and reported `>21 m/s` aggressive flight. Local HTTP Range extraction now parses all 36 `_500hz_freq_sync.csv` files (`996104` telemetry rows): `13/36` flights reach at least `21 m/s`, the fastest sample is `21.853` m/s, and the strongest P99 speed is `21.259` m/s. At the README 21 m/s floor, runtime `racingQuad` X-axis drag is `4.88` N and required total thrust is `0.22x` configured max; its inferred KV is `1.16x` the RATM 2020KV motor, while per-motor current limit is `0.41x` the RATM 55A ESC rating.
- The RATM acceleration/drag residual packet adds 642 `ratm_accel_drag_packet_*` rows from the six fastest 1 s windows. Runtime drag at each window's vmax implies median `4.65 m/s^2` drag-only deceleration, while median observed absolute speed-rate at vmax is `5.24 m/s^2`; across the same windows, current drag-decel P95 is `0.08x` observed-decel P95. This is not a passive drag fit, but it confirms the corrected runtime force law is in the same order as the powered-flight speed-rate envelope instead of overwhelming it.
- The RATM thrust-vector feasibility packet adds 205 `ratm_thrust_vector_packet_*` rows from the same windows. Across `827` samples at or above `21 m/s`, the high-speed command-projection proxy median is `0.69x` the corrected drag/max-thrust demand; at the six vmax samples, the median proxy is `0.42x`. Treat this as a sign/scale guard for attitude and thrust semantics, not as evidence that base drag alone blocks the logged speed.
- Blackbird and AI-IO add rotor-speed/IMU/mocap flight-log anchors below the RATM/UZH racing envelope. Blackbird exposes motor RPM/PWM, 100 Hz IMU, ~190 Hz motor-speed, and 360 Hz mocap for trajectories up to `7.0` m/s; the local Blackbird inventory packet parses `166` README preview links and `14` official downloader file/schema rows, but sample raw CSV probes currently return HTTP `502`. The new mirror probe adds current download-status evidence: the official root plus four raw CSV probes are still `502`, `7` open GitHub issues mention download/server/link/access problems, and the reachable Academic Torrents metadata lists `747` files / `4.7896 TB` but `0` CSV or rotor/PWM/state/groundTruth filename matches. Blackbird therefore remains a retry/mirror-status lead rather than a residual-force fit. AI-IO adds bidirectional-DShot rotor speed, BMI270 IMU, and VICON with high-speed manual flight up to `14.0` m/s. Current `racingQuad` X-axis drag at those speeds is `8.942`/`35.770` N, or `0.17x`/`0.68x` its horizontal thrust margin; these are useful for trajectory/RPM response validation even though they are not direct drag fits.
- The IDSIA Nano-Quadrotor/Crazyflie 2.1 Brushless system-ID packet adds a clean 100 Hz motor-rad/s/full-state source: `docs/data/nanodrone_sysid_packet.csv` has `1092` rows mirrored as `nanodrone_sysid_packet_*`, backed by `15` Git LFS CSVs / `75,096` samples / `750.81 s`. Its source `Kt = 3.72e-08 N/(rad/s)^2` matches the body-z specific-force proxy well (`R2 = 0.958`, all-data fitted `Kt = 3.716e-08`, train-fit/test `R2 = 0.953`), so it is a strong motor-unit and `omega^2` thrust-semantics check. Its torque proxy fits are weak and coordinate-sensitive (`0.077x/0.038x/-0.566x` source coefficient ratios), so use those rows as motor-order/implementation caveats, not direct FPV torque calibration.
- Local AI-IO HDF5 `test` splits are now fully discovered from the v1.0 archive into `docs/data/aiio_flight_log_sample_reference.csv` (`22` slices). The manual high `seq_1/test` slice has `2513` samples at `100` Hz, max speed `4.727` m/s, and max `rotor_spd` `21511` reported units. The fastest parsed sample is `AIIO_manual_high_seq_4_test` at `13.597` m/s; current `racingQuad` X drag at that sample vmax is `33.742` N (`0.64x` horizontal margin). The highest parsed `rotor_spd` is `29147` in `AIIO_manual_high_seq_2_test`, about `1.000x` current `racingQuad` max RPM if interpreted as mechanical RPM.
- `docs/data/neurobem_source_inventory.csv` adds a 120-row metadata packet for NeuroBEM: `95` flights, `13` test-set segments, `400 Hz` state, `0.772 kg` mass, motor-speed columns in rad/s, residual-force columns `36..38`, and residual-torque columns `39..41`. The updated `docs/data/neurobem_drag_residual_packet.csv` scans the public `predictions.tar.xz`: `251` CSV files, `1,816,329` rows, `76.05` min, body-speed sample P95/max `11.74/17.72 m/s`, residual-force P95 `0.915 N` (`0.121x` NeuroBEM weight), residual-torque P50/P95/max `0.00419/0.02276/0.1757 N*m`, and 0.1-scaled battery P50/P05 `15.33/14.30 V`. Its torque P95 is `0.650x` current `racingQuad` propwash max torque, and its equivalent angular-damping P95 is `0.0123 N*m/(rad/s)`, `0.684x` current baseline angular drag. The packet now carries `17293` rows, including per-file `Flights.txt` joins, all `13` official test-set flags, speed bins, trajectory-family summaries, and target-velocity summaries; target-velocity `1.6`/`2.4 m/s` groups have torque P95 `0.0391/0.0380 N*m`. Treat NeuroBEM as a residual-structure source, not as total drag or high-speed racing-envelope evidence.
- Passive coastdown makes the drag gap visible: from 20 to 5 m/s, the IMAV mass-fit `racingQuad` reference takes `7.598` s and `82.212` m, while current X/Z drag slows in `0.904`/`0.894` s over `8.356`/`8.265` m. Initial 20 m/s decel is `18.2x`/`18.4x` the IMAV fit.
- Against the same RPG linear rotor-drag shape, `racingQuad` current X-axis 20 to 5 m/s passive coastdown time is `0.355x` the RPG-derived time, with `6.10x` the initial 20 m/s deceleration. That comparison is less severe than IMAV body-drag, but still shows the current damping is strong.
- `docs/data/airframe_drag_calibration_packet.csv` now mirrors 288 `airframe_drag_packet_*` rows into the global summary. The packet adds WAVELab Pelican system-ID context (`54` Vicon/motor flights) and Manchester manoeuvrability thesis uncertainty anchors (`+/-6%` flight-vs-wind-tunnel drag coefficient, `+/-20%` drag build-up confidence interval), while keeping APdrone powered GPS decel rows as non-fit caveats.
- Even inside the IMAV speed range, a 12.5 to 2.5 m/s passive coastdown gives `racingQuad` X-axis current time/distance `1.929` s / `9.701` m versus IMAV `8.821` s / `54.808` m, so the large drag gap is not only a 20 m/s extrapolation artifact.
- In the current hybrid gust model, a representative `wind=10 m/s, dirtyAir=1.5` case gives target gust RMS of `1.653` m/s horizontal X and `0.843` m/s vertical after combining a scaled dirty-air burble with the low-altitude Dryden target. Against a Dryden reference at 6 m using the same 10 m/s wind, those are `0.86x` longitudinal and `0.84x` vertical turbulence intensity.
- The same wind case shows a spectral-shape caveat: current `gust_time_constant=0.116` s gives a one-pole corner near `1.373` Hz, while Dryden's low-altitude longitudinal/vertical poles are `0.037`/`0.265` Hz. At 1 Hz, the current one-pole shape is `21.9x` the Dryden longitudinal magnitude and `1.86x` the Dryden vertical magnitude, so the model can match RMS while still being too high-frequency.
- ICAS 2020 hover CFD shows a `10 m/s` gust can dominate rotor thrust: at 4319 rpm, CT changes from `-131%` for -90 deg downdraft to `+120%` for 90 deg updraft; at 6528 rpm the same endpoints are `-68%` and `+42%`. This supports keeping wind kinematics separate from direct rotor-inflow/thrust perturbations.
- `docs/data/wind_gust_calibration_packet.csv` now mirrors 632 `wind_gust_packet_*` rows into the global summary. It keeps current-vs-Dryden intensity rows, spectral-shape rows, ICAS hover-gust CT rows, and crosscheck metrics in one handoff table so the other agent can separate atmospheric turbulence, deterministic dirty-air feel, and rotor thrust perturbation.
- ICAS 2020 heavy-rain CFD at `LWC=19 g/m^3` gives CT losses `2.64%`/`1.67%` at 4319/6528 rpm. The older generated precipitation reference still carries `5.50%` full-wetness thrust loss (`2.08x`/`3.29x` ICAS), while current `DronePhysics.java` parses as `clamp(1 - 0.03 * wetness^0.85, 0.96, 1)`, or `3.00%` full-wetness loss (`1.14x`/`1.79x` ICAS).
- `docs/data/precipitation_water_packet.csv` now mirrors 1608 `precip_water_packet_*` rows into the global summary. The packet keeps rain mass-flux scans, moist-air-density rows, ICAS heavy-rain CT rows, water-immersion scans, and a current-source formula audit so stale generated rain coefficients are visible.
- The MDPI APT70-style hovering-rotor icing packet adds 362 `icing_rotor_packet_*` rows from Villeneuve et al. 2022. Table 4 cases at `4950 rpm`, `11.7 deg`, and `lambda=80 g/dm^2/h` project CT losses of `9.13..23.96%` over `106..761 s`, with required-power `P+` endpoint projections of `20.87..89.49%`. Those CT losses are `3.04..7.99x` the current full-rain `3.00%` loss, so these rows should seed a separate time-accumulating icing model rather than the ordinary rain wetness curve.
- `racingQuad` now carries `RotorSpec.bladeCount = 3` for blade-pass vibration and gyro notch telemetry. Its configured hover/max blade-pass frequencies are `651.155/1457` Hz, matching the three-blade FPV prop references at the same RPM.
- The UAV Realistic Fault Dataset adds `99` `SensorCombined.jsonl` missions across 0-4 broken-prop classes. Aggregating up to `3` sorted missions per class, the strongest median gyro dynamic-RMS ratio is class `4` at `2.34x` class 0, and the strongest median accelerometer dynamic-RMS ratio is class `4` at `7.41x`; use this as a real flight-phase-inclusive fault/noise envelope, not a steady hover calibration.
- The same repository's raw `Imu.jsonl` messages add frame-id-specific local vibration anchors without timestamps. Across up to `2` files per class, the strongest raw-IMU median gyro RMS ratio is class `2` at `1.06x` class 0, and the strongest raw-IMU median accel RMS ratio is class `3` at `1.52x`; use it as sensor-placement/local-vibration evidence, not a drop-in sample-rate-calibrated IMU noise source.
- Sampling one `AudioBuffer.jsonl` mission per UAV Realistic class adds raw microphone-payload amplitude anchors. The strongest sampled payload RMS ratio is class `4` at `1.03x` class 0, with block-RMS median ratio `0.96x`; treat these as dataset-internal audio features, not calibrated dB.
- The DronePropB sampled ground-test packet adds `111` public `.mat` file inventory rows and `12` representative C3 downloads in `docs/data/dronepropb_sample_packet.csv` (`1195` rows mirrored as `dronepropb_sample_packet_*`). In that subset, healthy `SP3` is already `3.30x` healthy `SP2` external-accelerometer dynamic RMS, while selected `SP2` fault samples have median/max RMS ratios `1.20x/1.49x` versus healthy `SP2`; dominant C3 peaks split around `~101 Hz` and `~590 Hz`. Treat speed/channel normalization as mandatory before fitting damage intensity.
- The DronePropB stratified expansion adds `26` selected files and `774` rows in `docs/data/dronepropb_stratified_vibration_packet.csv` (`dronepropb_stratified_packet_*`). For `21` fault rows normalized to healthy files at the same speed/channel, external-accelerometer RMS ratios are median/P90/max `1.184x/1.488x/2.246x`; the strongest selected row is `F3_SV2_SP3_C3.mat`. At fixed `SV2/C3`, the high-speed `SP3` group has median/max `1.808x/2.246x`, while fixed `SV2/SP2` channel medians range from `1.034x` to `1.320x`, so speed and sensor placement remain first-class conditioning variables.
- Full-file analysis of the DJI Mini 2 propeller-damage vibration dataset puts the healthy dominant vector-PSD peak near `159.678` Hz and fault vector dynamic-RMS ratios versus healthy from `0.96x` to `1.15x`. This is a real fault-signature anchor, but not a direct FPV blade-pass calibration because the dataset's `1024` Hz sample rate cannot resolve the current `racingQuad` hover blade-pass at `651.155` Hz without aliasing.
- The PADRE UAV measurement repository adds `587` public CSV files across `2` vehicles. In the sampled 3DR Solo FFT ACCEL_X/Y/Z subset, the strongest fault label `2010` has combined feature RMS `3.13x` healthy, giving a second prop-fault vibration feature-scale anchor independent of the DJI Mini 2 dataset.
- At the DJI dataset sample rate, `racingQuad` hover blade-pass `651.155` Hz aliases to `372.387` Hz, and max blade-pass `1457` Hz aliases to `433.340` Hz. Those alias peaks are not physical BPF matches, so use this dataset for fault signatures and amplitude/band-ratio sanity, not notch-frequency fitting.
- `docs/data/propeller_damage_vibration_packet.csv` now mirrors 469 `prop_damage_packet_*` rows into the global summary. It keeps UAV Realistic fault aggregates, DJI raw vibration spectra, PADRE FFT feature ratios, current rotor-damage scan rows, and current blade-pass alias rows in one handoff table.
- `racingQuad` configured gyro noise `0.025` rad/s is about `20.9x` an MPU-6000/6050 one-pole 120 Hz RMS estimate and `37.3x` an ICM-42688-P estimate. Treat the configured noise as frame vibration plus electronics, not bare IMU noise.
- `racingQuad` quiet barometer model noise is about `0.0059` m RMS from the accelerometer-noise coupling term, comparable to good MEMS pressure-sensor noise floors such as `Infineon DPS310` at `0.0166` m. But the modeled aligned-flow dynamic-pressure error at 20 m/s is `-1.004` m, so barometer realism is dominated by static-port/propwash pressure error rather than silicon pressure noise.
- The public Betaflight 4.2.4 blackbox log header has `looptime=125 us`, `pid_process_denom=2`, `dshot_bidir=1`, and an estimated main-log rate of `4000` Hz. Its field list has gyro, accelerometer, and motor command data, but no `eRPM` field, so it is a format/timing anchor rather than a motor-RPM validation log.
- `racingQuad` roll/pitch max rate is `720` deg/s, above Betaflight's common race-rate band (`550-650 deg/s`) but below its common freestyle band (`850-1200 deg/s`). The current curve's center slope is only `257` deg/s per stick because `rateSuper` preserves full-stick max while softening center authority.
- Betaflight's current blackbox source logs `eRPM / 100` when DShot telemetry fields are present. For a 14-pole motor, one logged count equals `14.29` mechanical rpm; the current `racingQuad` hover/max RPM would appear as about `912/2040` in an `eRPM[]` blackbox column.
- Decoding Betaflight PR #12562's `rpm_bb_stress_002` log with `orangebox` yields `27.6` s and `87279` frames of `RPM[0..3]` data. Interpreted through the log's `12`-pole header, all-motor median/max mechanical RPM are `24817/42917`, so the current `racingQuad` max RPM `29138` sits inside the public Betaflight RPM-log magnitude range.
- On that same stress log, the strongest decoded 50 ms positive RPM slew is `503271` rpm/s, or `0.78x` the current `racingQuad` first-order `maxRPM/motor_tau` proxy. This puts `motor_tau=0.0450 s` in the right order for aggressive Betaflight RPM changes, while the active-braking tau proxy remains much faster than the observed negative-slew maxima.
- The RPM-frequency table converts decoded mechanical RPM to motor harmonics and three-blade blade-pass. `racingQuad` hover/max blade-pass is `651`/`1457` Hz; PR #12562 `rpm_bb_stress_002` three-blade-equivalent P95/max reaches `2083`/`2146` Hz, so the current max BPF is `0.68x` the decoded max-H3 band. Treat this as frequency-range sanity, not same-prop proof.
- The PR #12562 stress log's decoded gyro spectrum is dominated by low-frequency motion/noise: vector RMS in `5-60 Hz` is `65.276` gyro units, while the +/-10 Hz band around the decoded max three-blade harmonic alias at `1029` Hz is only `0.049`. Use these logs for RPM telemetry/response and alias bookkeeping, not as a flight propwash vibration fit.

## Rotor forward-flow model sanity

Generated forward-flow CSV: `docs/data/rotor_forward_flow_reference.csv`. The key unit warning is that UIUC's propeller advance ratio is `J = V/(nD)`, while the Java code's `rotorAdvanceRatio` is `mu = V/(omega R) = J/pi`; comparing the raw values directly would be off by a factor of pi.
Generated J/mu guard packet CSV: `docs/data/uiuc_forward_flow_mu_guard_packet.csv`. It adds `1696` narrow metrics for UIUC 5-inch fits, current level-forward points, current threshold mappings, APC axial high-J boundaries, and the Mejzlik wind-tunnel table. These rows are mirrored into `docs/data/fpv_model_validation_summary.csv` as `uiuc_mu_guard_packet_*` categories.

|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| 0.25 | 0.080 | 0.905 | 0.968 | 1.063 | 0.853/0.979 | 0.815/1.174 |
| 0.45 | 0.143 | 0.549 | 0.688 | 1.254 | 0.517/0.592 | 0.586/0.774 |
| 0.65 | 0.207 | 0.193 | 0.409 | 2.471 | 0.099/0.299 | 0.356/0.496 |

| `racingQuad` level speed | code mu / UIUC J | UIUC CT ratio fit | UIUC CP ratio fit | UIUC Q/T ratio | current airflow multiplier | code/UIUC CT | power proxy/UIUC CP | disk drag per rotor | flap tilt | rotor stall |
|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| 5.0 m/s | 0.058 / 0.181 | 1.028 | 1.064 | 1.028 | 1.009 | 0.98x | 0.95x | 0.031 N | 0.40 deg | 0.000 |
| 10.0 m/s | 0.115 / 0.363 | 0.705 | 0.810 | 1.146 | 1.040 | 1.48x | 1.28x | 0.125 N | 0.79 deg | 0.000 |

Low-precision STARMAC II Fig. 9 digitization source: [Quadrotor Helicopter Flight Dynamics and Control](https://ai.stanford.edu/~gabeh/papers/Quadrotor_Dynamics_GNC07.pdf). The paper figure compares measured blade deflection against stiff-blade and hinged-blade predictions; use the rows below as a flapping scale check, not a high-accuracy fit target.

| Wind speed | measured deflection | stiff-blade prediction | hinged-blade prediction | `racingQuad` same-speed flap proxy | `racingQuad` mu |
|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| 0.0 m/s | 0.00 deg | 0.00 deg | 0.00 deg | 0.00 deg | 0.000 |
| 0.6 m/s | 0.14 deg | 0.16 deg | 0.85 deg | 0.05 deg | 0.007 |
| 1.1 m/s | 0.30 deg | 0.32 deg | 1.55 deg | 0.09 deg | 0.013 |
| 1.5 m/s | 0.45 deg | 0.45 deg | 2.15 deg | 0.12 deg | 0.017 |
| 1.8 m/s | 0.58 deg | 0.57 deg | 2.60 deg | 0.14 deg | 0.021 |
| 2.5 m/s | 0.82 deg | 0.80 deg | 3.65 deg | 0.20 deg | 0.029 |
| 3.4 m/s | 1.12 deg | 1.10 deg | 4.95 deg | 0.27 deg | 0.039 |

At the 12.5 m/s `racingQuad` proxy, the equivalent UIUC `J` is close to the common 0.45 comparison point: the 5-inch prop fits predict roughly half static CT and lower same-RPM CP, while the current steady airflow multiplier and same-RPM constant-Q/T power proxy are still above 1 because translational-lift boost dominates and the high-advance loss does not start until `mu = 0.46` (`J about 1.45`). If this is intended as physical forward-flight propeller behavior rather than gameplay assist, the rolloff threshold likely needs recalibration against `J`, not raw `mu`.

High-advance axial propeller packet: `docs/scripts/analyze_high_advance_rotor_prop_sources.py` downloads APC performance files and generates `docs/data/apc_high_advance_propeller_reference.csv` (`7590` rows), `docs/data/high_advance_rotor_source_inventory.csv` (`16` rows), and `docs/data/high_advance_rotor_prop_packet.csv` (`637` rows mirrored as `high_advance_packet_*`). APC rows are axial `J` predictions from actual prop geometry, not edgewise rotor `mu` measurements; use them to extend axial CT/CP shape checks beyond UIUC, and use NASA/UMD/DLR rotor sources for retreating-blade-stall phenomenology.

| 5.1x5.0E 3-blade | 1.130 | 0.360 | 0.360 | FPV-adjacent three-blade reference |
| 5x7.5E | 1.708 | 0.544 | 0.542 | high-pitch bridge toward current stall onset |
| 5x11E | 2.466 | 0.785 | 0.781 | extreme-pitch high-J coverage near current upper range |

## Rotor blade dissymmetry and retreating-blade stall sanity

Generated blade-dissymmetry CSV: `docs/data/rotor_blade_dissymmetry_reference.csv`. This section uses the code's `mu = V/(omega R)` convention directly. The simple reverse-flow proxy is `r/R < mu` on the retreating side, so it is a geometric warning flag, not a complete stall model.

| Reference | advance-ratio anchor | Use | Source |
|---|---:|---|---|
| FAA Helicopter Flying Handbook | qualitative | FAA handbook source for retreating-blade-stall symptoms and high-speed/high-load contributors; qualitative anchor only. | [source](https://www.faa.gov/sites/faa.gov/files/regulations_policies/handbooks_manuals/aviation/helicopter_flying_handbook/hfh_ch11.pdf) |
| NASA CR-2008-215370 high advance ratio rotor review | mu 0.00-1.00 | NASA rotorcraft report reviewing performance data and theory at high advance ratio, including operation approaching mu=1. | [source](https://rotorcraft.arc.nasa.gov/Publications/files/NASA%20CR%202008-215370%20Harris.pdf) |
| UH-60A slowed rotor high-advance-ratio tests | mu 0.30-1.00 | NASA/Army high-advance-ratio slowed-rotor testing; useful for the mu range where reverse flow and stall become major rotor phenomena. | [source](https://rotorcraft.arc.nasa.gov/Publications/files/A-6-F_Kottapalli.pdf) |
| DLR ERF2023 dynamic-stall rotor-code validation | mu 0.40 | DLR paper uses model-rotor measurements at mu=0.4 to validate dynamic-stall computation. | [source](https://elib.dlr.de/191749/1/vanderWall%20-%20ERF2023_0001_vanderWall.pdf) |

| neighboring high-advance loss starts/full | 0.46 / 0.92 | separate high-advance thrust-loss gate |

For `racingQuad`, the current hover-RPM retreating-stall onset speed is about `36.372` m/s and the full-stall point about `71.012` m/s. At max RPM those move to `81.378` and `158.880` m/s. That makes the current curve mainly a low-throttle/high-forward-speed or unloaded-rotor edge case for a fast FPV quad, not a normal hover-throttle cruise effect.

## Prop pitch geometry sanity

Sources: official HQProp/Gemfan product pages reused from the physical prop-mass packet. Generated prop-geometry CSV: `docs/data/prop_geometry_pitch_reference.csv`. Current presets without an explicit `withRotorBladePitchMeters(...)` override use Java's `RotorSpec.defaultBladePitchMeters(radius) = max(0.01, 1.70R)`, which is equivalent to `P/D = 0.85` except for very small radii hitting the 10 mm floor.

Generated prop-pitch packet CSV: `docs/data/prop_pitch_geometry_packet.csv`. It condenses 294 `prop_pitch_packet_*` rows into current presets, official HQProp/Gemfan pitch/mass references, UIUC 70%R geometry summaries, current-vs-official ratios, current-vs-UIUC ratios, and crosscheck rows mirrored into `docs/data/fpv_model_validation_summary.csv`.

| Prop-pitch packet item | value | read as |
|---|---:|---|
| default current P/D range | `0.85..0.85` | every current preset uses the same default |
| official prop references | `8` | HQProp/Gemfan 5in/3in/10in anchors |
| UIUC geometry station rows | `126` | raw `r/R`, `c/R`, `beta` source rows |
| racing official pitch ratio | `0.85..1.18x` | acceptable 5in proxy |
| racing UIUC 70%R angle ratio | `1.01..1.22x` | 5in pitch angle close |
| racing UIUC 70%R chord ratio | `0.58..0.89x` | chord proxy can be low |
| heavy official pitch ratio | `1.70..1.89x` | large-lift default pitch too high |
| heavy UIUC 70%R angle ratio | `1.18..1.86x` | heavy pitch angle too high vs 10in geometry |
| heavy UIUC local P/D ratio | `1.19..1.92x` | per-preset pitch override recommended |

The fixed default pitch is a decent first-order 5-inch FPV proxy: `racingQuad` same-size comparisons span `0.85..1.18x` reference pitch. It is much less plausible as a universal large-prop default: `heavyLift` becomes `1.70..1.89x` official 10-inch Gemfan pitch, so model paths using pitch speed, windmilling reverse axial speed, chord/Re proxy, or geometric stall angle should get per-preset prop pitch rather than inheriting `P/D=0.85`.

| [RotorPy Hummingbird](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/spencerfolk/rotorpy/main/rotorpy/vehicles/hummingbird_params.py) | 4 | 0.500 kg | 0.004/0.004/0.007 | n/a m | 5.570e-06 | 0.0244 | 1500 | 10.22 | 0.313 | n/a/n/a s | n/a | 0.005/0.005/0.010 |

RotorS and PX4 use the same simple thrust form as this project, `T = k * omega^2`. The `T/W max` and `hover omega/max` columns are derived from each source's mass, rotor count, motor constant, and max rotor velocity; they are useful thrust-margin checks, while normalized CT remains a geometry-dependent sanity range.

gym-pybullet-drones also exposes simple ground-effect and multi-drone downwash formulas in `BaseAviary.py`: extra ground-effect force is proportional to `rpm^2 * kf * gnd_eff_coeff * (R / (4h))^2`, and downwash uses `alpha = dw1 * (R / (4 dz))^2`, `beta = dw2 * dz + dw3`, then a Gaussian lateral falloff. Those formulas are useful references for this project's ground, propwash, and nearby-drone wake terms.

## Airframe inertia sanity

The table compares radius of gyration `r = sqrt(I/m)` instead of raw inertia. This makes a 27 g Crazyflie, a 1.5 kg Iris, and the current presets comparable on geometry rather than mass. For the yaw ratio, current project presets use their vertical `Y` axis, while URDF/SDF/Python open models use their source `Z` axis.

Current 5-inch and small-lift presets are in the same mass-normalized geometry range as RotorS Hummingbird and PX4 Iris. The larger lift presets have larger radii of gyration, as expected from longer arms and battery/payload mass farther from the center.

## Body drag sanity

Current code path: `linearDragCoefficient` contributes linear damping `F = -k * v` in world axes, while `bodyDragCoefficients` contribute per-axis quadratic drag `F_i = -c_i * v_i * |v_i|` in body axes before separated-flow additions. The values below assume sea-level density ratio and do not include the separated-flow term; equivalent `CdA` is therefore speed-specific when linear damping is present. Drag and flight-envelope anchors: [IMAV 2022 quadrotor drag paper](https://www.imavs.org/papers/2022/4.pdf) reports `D = kV`, `k = 0.105 + 0.087*m`, for a 5-inch three-blade quadrotor; [UZH-FPV Drone Racing Dataset](https://fpv.ifi.uzh.ch/datasets/) provides public FPV racing sequence speeds and [ICRA 2019 paper context](https://rpg.ifi.uzh.ch/docs/ICRA19_Delmerico.pdf); [RATM](https://github.com/tii-racing/drone-racing-dataset), [Blackbird](https://github.com/mit-aera/Blackbird-Dataset), [AI-IO](https://github.com/SJTU-ViSYS-team/AI-IO), and [WAVELab Pelican](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/wavelab/pelican_dataset/master/README.md) provide trajectory/RPM/IMU/system-identification data; [Manchester manoeuvrability thesis](https://research.manchester.ac.uk/en/studentTheses/theoretical-and-practical-limits-on-multi-rotor-manoeuvrability/) provides open drag-test method and uncertainty context; [NASA multicopter wind-tunnel paper](https://rotorcraft.arc.nasa.gov/Publications/files/72-2016-374.pdf) gives small-UAS wind-tunnel speed/dynamic-pressure context; [NASA drag equation](https://www1.grc.nasa.gov/beginners-guide-to-aeronautics/drag-equation/) is used for equivalent `CdA`; [RotorPy Hummingbird](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/spencerfolk/rotorpy/main/rotorpy/vehicles/hummingbird_params.py) uses direct quadratic `c_D` in `N/(m/s)^2`; [UZH/RPG FPV controller parameters](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/uzh-rpg/rpg_quadrotor_control/master/control/position_controller/parameters/fpv.yaml) and the [rotor-drag flatness paper](http://rpg.ifi.uzh.ch/docs/RAL18_Faessler.pdf) provide mass-normalized linear rotor-drag coefficients; [ICAS 2020 quadrotor adverse-situations CFD](https://www.icas.org/icas_archive/ICAS2020/data/papers/ICAS2020_0482_paper.pdf) provides forward-flight and freefall drag tables.

Generated airframe-drag CSV: `docs/data/airframe_drag_reference.csv`. It converts IMAV's linear low-speed fit, UZH-FPV speed-envelope rows, RATM/Blackbird/AI-IO flight-log context rows, NASA wind-tunnel speed points, open-source quadratic coefficients, RPG linear rotor-drag coefficients, ICAS CFD forward/freefall drag tables, and current presets into common `force`, `effective linear k`, equivalent `CdA`, and passive coastdown fields.
Generated NASA bare-airframe digitization CSV: `docs/data/nasa_bare_airframe_drag_digitized_reference.csv`. NASA Fig. 30 reports bare-airframe `Drag/q` in ft^2; the generated rows convert it to SI equivalent `CdA` and this project's quadratic coefficient form.
Generated NASA powered full-airframe digitization CSV: `docs/data/nasa_powered_full_airframe_drag_digitized_reference.csv`. NASA Figs. 18/20/22 plot powered drag in lbf at `q=0.48 lb/ft^2`; the generated rows convert 0 deg points to N, equivalent `CdA`, and this project's quadratic coefficient form.
Generated NASA powered lift digitization CSV: `docs/data/nasa_powered_lift_digitized_reference.csv`. NASA Figs. 17/19/21 plot powered lift in lbf at `q=0.48 lb/ft^2`; the generated rows convert 0 deg points to N, effective `T/omega^2`, Table 1 `lift/weight`, and total-disk CT for RPM-scale checks.
RPG rotor-drag comparison rows map RPG horizontal `x/y` to this project's horizontal `X/Z`; RPG `z` maps to the project's vertical `Y` and is zero in the FPV parameter file.
Generated APdrone drag packet CSV: `docs/data/apdrone_drag_calibration_packet.csv`. It condenses the APdrone open-field speed envelope, GPS-event dynamics bins, and trim/deceleration filters into one narrow metric table and mirrors those metrics into `docs/data/fpv_model_validation_summary.csv` as `apdrone_drag_*` categories.
Generated airframe drag packet CSV: `docs/data/airframe_drag_calibration_packet.csv`. It condenses the source inventory, current racingQuad drag, IMAV/NASA/RPG comparisons, flight-envelope checks, APdrone log-fit caveats, AI-IO sample extremes, Pelican system-ID context, and Manchester manoeuvrability uncertainty anchors into `airframe_drag_packet_*` summary rows.
Generated airframe CdA guard packet CSV: `docs/data/airframe_cda_guard_packet.csv`. It narrows the drag evidence into coefficient-scale guardrails from IMAV, NASA, RotorPy, RPG, ICAS, RATM, APdrone, and Manchester, and mirrors them into `docs/data/fpv_model_validation_summary.csv` as `airframe_cda_guard_packet_*` rows.
Generated Blackbird mirror probe CSV: `docs/data/blackbird_mirror_probe_packet.csv`. It mirrors `58` `blackbird_mirror_probe_packet_*` rows and confirms that the currently reachable Academic Torrents mirror is not a raw CSV/RPM/mocap source for drag fitting.

| APdrone open-field GPS max | `18.72 m/s` |
| `16-20 m/s` speed-bin apparent decel P50 | `0.0111 N/(m/s)^2` / `0.091x` `apDrone()` X |
| `straight_decel_v_ge_16` | `3` events, P50 diagnostic coeff `0.00841 N/(m/s)^2` / `0.069x` `apDrone()` X |

APdrone open-field logs do not remove attitude, wind, or horizontal thrust, so this packet is evidence for envelope feasibility and non-fit warnings, not a final airframe `CdA` calibration.

Against that NASA small-quad bare-airframe median, runtime `racingQuad` X-axis base drag at 10 m/s is `2.050` N, `1.60x` the wind-tunnel bare-frame median. Because NASA's figure excludes powered rotor/body interactions, use it as a lower-bound body-drag anchor rather than a complete forward-flight drag target.

Against that NASA powered full-airframe median, current `racingQuad` X-axis base drag at `6.126` m/s is `6.848` N, `4.3x` the wind-tunnel powered median. The full CSV keeps all 15 RPM points; the table uses one middle-RPM point per vehicle to avoid over-weighting the RPM sweep.

NASA powered lift digitization, mid-RPM 0 deg points:

| 3DR Iris+ Fig. 21 | 0.48 lb/ft^2 | 6.126 m/s | 5400 | 2.92 lbf / 12.989 N | 1.04 | 0.012 | 1.015e-05 |
| small-quad mid-RPM median | 0.48 lb/ft^2 | 6.126 m/s | 5400 | 3.43 lbf / 15.257 N | 1.14 | 0.012 | 1.170e-05 |

At the NASA lift median RPM, current `racingQuad` total static thrust would be `1.855` N, only `0.12x` that NASA median lift. Reaching the same total lift with current `racingQuad` thrust coefficient would need about `15488` RPM, `0.53x` configured max RPM. This mainly documents prop/vehicle scale separation between NASA COTS quads and a 5-inch racing preset.

| cinewhoop | z | y | 20.0 -> 5.0 m/s | 3.591 s / 38.860 m | 3.266 s / 33.418 m | 0.909x | 0.860x | 1.47x |
| heavyLift | x | x | 20.0 -> 5.0 m/s | 2.548 s / 27.574 m | 12.366 s / 127.121 m | 4.853x | 4.610x | 0.27x |
| heavyLift | z | y | 20.0 -> 5.0 m/s | 3.591 s / 38.860 m | 10.697 s / 108.390 m | 2.978x | 2.789x | 0.47x |

The important warning is formula-level: `linearDragCoefficient` is runtime linear damping in `N/(m/s)`, while `bodyDragCoefficients` are quadratic body-axis terms. For `racingQuad`, the combined runtime force lands close to the IMAV mass-fit coastdown at low speed, but its speed-specific equivalent `CdA` decreases as speed rises because the linear term is being projected into `F=cV^2`. Physical CdA fitting, rotor-drag shaping, and gameplay damping should therefore stay as separate model surfaces.

## Standard atmosphere, Reynolds, and tip Mach sanity

References: [NASA standard atmosphere](https://www.grc.nasa.gov/www/k-12/airplane/atmosmet.html), [NASA speed of sound](https://www.grc.nasa.gov/www/BGH/sound.html), [NASA Sutherland viscosity model](https://www.grc.nasa.gov/www/BGH/viscosity.html), [U.S. Standard Atmosphere 1976](https://ntrs.nasa.gov/citations/19770009539), and the UIUC Reynolds-number propeller reference listed in the source packet. Generated atmosphere CSV: `docs/data/atmosphere_reynolds_mach_summary.csv`.

The table mirrors the current Java formulas for standard-atmosphere pressure ratio, density ratio, speed of sound, and Sutherland-law dynamic viscosity. The `Re75` column is a proxy using 75% span speed and a representative chord of `0.12R` scaled by the project's pitch/chord proxy; the `code Re index` and `low-Re loss` columns mirror the current low-Reynolds model path more directly.
